     function reset(res){
try{
document.getElementById(res[0]+"_1_"+"t").style.color="#000"
}catch(e){
}
try{
document.getElementById(res[0]+"_1_"+"f").style.color="#000"
}catch(e){
}try{
document.getElementById(res[0]+"_2_"+"t").style.color="#000"
}catch(e){
}try{
document.getElementById(res[0]+"_2_"+"f").style.color="#000"
}catch(e){
}try{
document.getElementById(res[0]+"_3_"+"t").style.color="#000"
}catch(e){
}try{
document.getElementById(res[0]+"_3_"+"f").style.color="#000"
}catch(e){
}try{
document.getElementById(res[0]+"_4_"+"t").style.color="#000"
}catch(e){
}try{
document.getElementById(res[0]+"_4_"+"f").style.color="#000"
}catch(e){
}

document.getElementById(res[0]+"_answ").style.display='none';
document.getElementById(res[0]+"_ansc").style.display='none';
document.getElementById(res[0]+"_answerText").style.display='none';
}
function testMulti(element){


id=element.id;
var res = id.split("_"); 
reset(res);
if(res[2]=="t"){
document.getElementById(element.id).style.color="#1EA303"
document.getElementById(res[0]+"_answ").style.display='none';
document.getElementById(res[0]+"_ansc").style.display='block';
var idnumber=res[0]+"_answerText"
 $("#"+idnumber).show('slow');
}else{
document.getElementById(element.id).style.color="#F60E02"
document.getElementById(res[0]+"_answ").style.display='block';
document.getElementById(res[0]+"_ansc").style.display='none';
var idnumber=res[0]+"_answerText"
 $("#"+idnumber).hide('slow');
}
//document.getElementById(res[0]+"_answerText").style.display='block';


}

  <script type="text/javascript">
      //<![CDATA[
      var classicMode = false ;
      var summary = 30;
      var indent = 3;
      function stripHtmlTags(s,max){return s.replace(/<.*?>/ig, '').split(/\s+/).slice(0,max-1).join(' ')}
      function getSummaryLikeWP(id) {
        return document.getElementById(id).innerHTML.split(/<!--\s*more\s*-->/)[0];
      }
      function getSummaryImproved(post,max){
        var re = /<.*?>/gi
        var re2 = /<br.*?>/gi
        var re3 = /(<\/{1}p>)|(<\/{1}div>)/gi
        var re4 = /(<style.*?\/{1}style>)|(<script.*?\/{1}script>)|(<table.*?\/{1}table>)|(<form.*?\/{1}form>)|(<code.*?\/{1}code>)|(<pre.*?\/{1}pre>)/gi
        post = post.replace(re4,'')
        post = post.replace(re3,'<br /> ').split(re2)
        for(var i=0; i<post.length; i++){
          post[i] = post[i].replace(re,'');
        }
        var post2 = new Array();
        for(var i in post) {
          //if(post[i]!='' && post[i]!=' ' && post[i] != '\n') post2.push(post[i]);
          if(/[a-zA-Z0-9]/.test(post[i])) post2.push(post[i]) ;
        }
        var s = "";
        var indentBlank = "";
        for(var i=0;i<indent;i++){
          indentBlank += " ";
        }
        if(post2.join('<br/>').split(' ').length < max-1 ){
          s = post2.join(indentBlank +' <br/>');
        } else {
          var i = 0;
          while(s.split(' ').length < max){
            s += indentBlank + ' ' + post2[i]+'<br/>';
            i++;
          }
        }
        return s;
      }
      function createSummaryAndThumb(pID,title,url,date,comment){
        var posturl= url;
        var title=title;
        var date =date;
        var comment = comment;
        var div = document.getElementById(pID);
        var content = div.innerHTML;
        if (/<!--\s*more\s*-->/.test(content)) {
          div.innerHTML = getSummaryLikeWP(pID);
          div.style.display = "block";
        }
        else {
          var imgtag = "";
          var img = div.getElementsByTagName("img");
          var summ = summary;
          if(img.length>=1) {
            imgtag = '<div class="post-thumbnail"><a href="'+posturl+'"><img width="215" height="150" class="thumbnail" src="'+img[0].src+'"><span class="overlay-icon"></span></a></div>';
          }
          var summary1 = imgtag+'<div class="entry"><p>'+stripHtmlTags(content,summary)+'... <a class="more-link" href="'+posturl+'">read more ?</a></p></div>';
          div.innerHTML = summary1;
          div.style.display = "block";
        }
      }
      //]]>
    </script>

                <h1 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name headline"> <a href="http://www.instanceofjava.com/2016/08/quicksort-example-in-java-recursion.html" itemprop="url"> Quicksort algorithm in java with example program </a> </h1> 
                <div class="clear"></div> 
                <p class="post-meta"> <span> Posted by: InstanceOfJava </span> <span> Posted date: <strong> Aug 16, 2016 </strong> </span> <span> / </span> <span class="meta_comments"> comment : 0 </span> </p> 
                <div class="post-body entry" id="post-body-8452739576925498460" itemprop="description articleBody"> 
                 <p> </p>
                 <div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on"> 
                  <ul style="text-align: left;"> 
                   <li>Quick sort uses divide and conquer algorithm.</li> 
                   <li>First will be divided in to two parts based on some pivot element. All elements which are less than pivot element will be placed left and and all elements which are greater than pivot will be in right part.</li> 
                   <div style="float: right;"> 
                    <script async src="//pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js"></script> 
                    <!-- corejava page ad --> 
                    <br> 
                    <ins class="adsbygoogle" data-ad-client="ca-pub-2870509575640354" data-ad-slot="7832511827" style="display: inline-block; height: 280px; width: 336px;"></ins>
                    <script>
(adsbygoogle = window.adsbygoogle || []).push({});
</script> 
                   </div> 
                   <li>So now pivot element is exactly in middle. if we sort left and right side elements all elements will be sorted. Here recursive quick sort will take place in order to sort all elements.</li> 
                   <li>Quick sort will be sorting these elements without using extra space that is the reason it is called <b>in place sorting algorithm.</b></li> 
                   <li>Using the first or middle elements as an pivot element. it splits the arrays by re arranging the elements like every thing that is less than pivot will come left side and all elements greater than or equal to pivot will come right side.</li> 
                   <li>Now pivot is in middle and correct place it left and right arrays sorted then entire array will be sorted.</li> 
                   <li>Quick sort exactly will do the same it will sort left and right recursively.</li> 
                   <li>If size of input is very&nbsp; less merge sort will be time consuming.</li> 
                   <li>For smaller inputs quick sort is faster than merge sort.</li> 
                   <li>Time complexity of Quicksort&nbsp; default case is O(n log n).</li> 
                   <li>Worst case Time complexity of&nbsp; Quicksort&nbsp; is O(n<sup>2</sup>).</li> 
                  </ul> 
                  <span style="color: #783f04;"><b>Steps to implement quick sort algorithm:&nbsp;</b></span>
                  <br> 
                  <br> 
                  <ul style="text-align: left;"> 
                   <li>Create a array with some elements. Choose pivot element as middle element. we can choose first or last also.</li> 
                   <li>After choosing pivot element arrange the elements like all elements which are less than pivot value comes left side and elements greater than equal to pivot come right side of pivot.</li> 
                   <li>And then apply same to both sides. until it becomes one. then all elements in array will be sorted.</li> 
                  </ul> 
                  <br> &nbsp;
                  <span style="color: #783f04;"><b>Program #1: Java Example program to sort elements of array using quick sort algorithm:</b></span>
                  <br> 
                  <br> 
                  <div class="program-div" style="text-align: left;"> 
                   <div class="dp-highlighter"> 
                    <ol class="dp-j"> 
                     <li class="alt">package quicksortjava;</li> 
                     <li class="alt"><br></li> 
                     <li class="alt">public class QuickSort {</li> 
                     <li class="alt"><span class="Apple-tab-span" style="white-space: pre;"> </span>&nbsp;</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; private int array[];</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; private int length;</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp;</li> 
                     <li class="alt">public void sortElements(int[] arrayvalues) {</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if (arrayvalues == null || arrayvalues.length == 0) {</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; return;</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; }</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; this.array = arrayvalues;</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; length = arrayvalues.length;</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; doQuickSort(0, length - 1);</li> 
                     <li class="alt">}</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp;</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; private void doQuickSort(int lowIndex, int highIndex) {</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; int i = lowIndex;</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; int j = highIndex;</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; int pivot = array[lowIndex+(highIndex-lowIndex)/2];</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // now Divide the array into two arrays(actually we are maintaining single array only)</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; while (i &lt;= j) {</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; <span class="Apple-tab-span" style="white-space: pre;"> </span></li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; while (array[i] &lt; pivot) {</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; i++;</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; }</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; while (array[j] &gt; pivot) {</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; j--;</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; }</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if (i &lt;= j) {</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; swapElements(i, j);</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; //move index to next position on both sides</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; i++;</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; j--;</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; }</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; }</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // call quickSort() method recursively</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if (lowIndex &lt; j){</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; <span class="Apple-tab-span" style="white-space: pre;"> </span></li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; <span class="Apple-tab-span" style="white-space: pre;"> </span>doQuickSort(lowIndex, j);</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; }</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if (i &lt; highIndex){</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; <span class="Apple-tab-span" style="white-space: pre;"> </span></li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; <span class="Apple-tab-span" style="white-space: pre;"> </span>doQuickSort(i, highIndex);</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; }</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; }</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp;</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</li> 
                     <li class="alt">private void swapElements(int i, int j) {</li> 
                     <li class="alt"><br></li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; int temp = array[i];</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; array[i] = array[j];</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; array[j] = temp;</li> 
                     <li class="alt"><br></li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp;}</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp;public static void main(String a[]){</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; <span class="Apple-tab-span" style="white-space: pre;"> </span>QuickSort quicksort = new QuickSort();</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; int[] inputarray = {32,1,23,14,43,7,6,65};</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; System.out.println("Before sorting");</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for(int i:inputarray){</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; System.out.print(i);</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; System.out.print(" ");</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; }</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp;quicksort.sortElements(inputarray);</li> 
                     <li class="alt"><br></li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; System.out.println("After sorting");</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; for(int i:inputarray){</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; System.out.print(i);</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; System.out.print(" ");</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; }</li> 
                     <li class="alt">&nbsp; &nbsp; }</li> 
                     <li class="alt"><br></li> 
                     <li class="alt">}</li> 
                    </ol> 
                   </div> 
                  </div> &nbsp;
                  <b><span style="color: #783f04;">Output:</span></b>
                  <br> 
                  <br> 
                  <div class="program-div" style="text-align: left;"> 
                   <div class="dp-highlighter"> 
                    <ol class="dp-j"> 
                     <li class="alt"></li> 
                     <li class="alt">Before sorting</li> 
                     <li class="alt">32 1 23 14 43 7 6 65&nbsp;</li> 
                     <li class="alt">After sorting</li> 
                     <li class="alt">1 6 7 14 23 32 43 65&nbsp;</li> 
                    </ol> 
                   </div> 
                  </div> 
                  <br> 
                  <span style="color: #783f04;"><b>Execution flow explanation of quick sort algorithm</b></span>
                  <br> 
                  <br> 
                  <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"> 
                   <a href="https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-eAb9DFuViRw/V7SFMx__2gI/AAAAAAAABNk/e4_4OpvzF2UYNHdhjwKc2oFejHEZ2XZqQCLcB/s1600/quick%2Bsort%2Bprogram%2Bin%2Bjava%2Busing%2Brecursion%2Bprogram.png" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img alt="quick sort program in java using recursion program" border="0" src="https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-eAb9DFuViRw/V7SFMx__2gI/AAAAAAAABNk/e4_4OpvzF2UYNHdhjwKc2oFejHEZ2XZqQCLcB/s1600/quick%2Bsort%2Bprogram%2Bin%2Bjava%2Busing%2Brecursion%2Bprogram.png" title="quick sort program in java using recursion program"></a>
                  </div> 
                  <br> 
                  <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"> 
                  </div> 
                  <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
